  1208. # [09:55] <nrc> jaws: just a quick question - do you remember doing the css for findBar?
  1209. # [09:55] <jaws> nrc: the animation? yes
  1210. # [09:56] <nrc> jaws: yeah, the transitions, why is the delay on [hidden] rather than the base css selector?
  1211. # [09:56] * Quits: sicking (sicking@moz-7F871C5C.hsd1.ca.comcast.net) (Quit: sicking)
  1212. # [09:56] <jaws> because we don't want to show the transition when switching tabs
  1213. # [09:56] <jaws> nrc: ^
  1214. # [09:56] <jaws> iirc, it may take me a few minutes to verify
  1215. # [09:57] <jaws> nrc: that's the wrong answer, i know why now
  1216. # [09:58] * Joins: marcoz (marco.zehe@moz-5503BDB7.dip0.t-ipconnect.de)
  1217. # [09:58] <jaws> nrc: it's because transition-delay defaults to 0s, in the case of showing it, we want to switch from visibility: collapse to visibility:visible immediately. but in the case of hiding, we want to delay switching from visibility:visible to visibility:collapse until after the other properties have finished their interpolation
  1218. # [09:59] <nrc> jaws: that makes sense, thank you!
  1219. # [09:59] <jaws> no problem! :)
